                        <script type="text/javascript">
                        // <![CDATA[

                        // Get country code from Universal Variable
                        function getUVCountyCode() {
                            if (window.universal_variable && window.universal_variable.user) {
                                var uv = window.universal_variable;
                                var countryCode = uv.user.country.toUpperCase();

                                return countryCode;

                            } else {

                                return false;

                            }
                        }

                        // Get server time from UV
                        function getUVServerTime() {
                            var dateTime = new Date(); // use client time if UV not available

                            if (window.universal_variable && window.universal_variable.servertime) {
                                var uv = window.universal_variable || {};
                                dateTime = uv.servertime;
                            }
                            return dateTime;
                        }

                        // get query parameter
                        // https://davidwalsh.name/query-string-javascript
                        function getUrlParameter(name) {
                            name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\\[').replace(/[\]]/, '\\]');
                            var regex = new RegExp('[\\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)');
                            var results = regex.exec(location.search);

                            return results === null ? '' : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
                        }
                        ;

                        // Get country code from country picker
                        (function($) {
                            $.fn.getPickerCountryCode = function() {
                                var scc = $(this).children(':selected').val();

                                return scc;
                            };
                        }(jQuery));

                        // Calculate millisecond time between two dates
                        function getTimeBetween(date1, date2) {

                            // Convert both dates to UTC milliseconds
                            var date1_ms = date1.getTime();
                            var date2_ms = date2.getTime();

                            // Calculate the difference in milliseconds
                            if (date1_ms < date2_ms) {
                                // today's date must be before the last delivery date

                                var difference_ms = Math.abs(date1_ms - date2_ms);

                            } else {

                                var difference_ms = 0;

                            }

                            return difference_ms;
                        }

                        // put all country codes from JSON data into array
                        (function($) {
                            $.fn.getJSONCountryCodes = function() {
                                var jcc = [];

                                $.each(christmasDeliveryData.countries, function(index, countries) {
                                    jcc.push(countries.country_code);
                                });

                                return jcc;
                            };
                        }(jQuery));

                        // convert to days, hours or minutes
                        function convertTime(milliseconds, unit) {

                            // the number of milliseconds in different units
                            var oneDay = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24;
                            var oneHour = 1000 * 60 * 60;
                            var oneMinute = 1000 * 60;
                            var converted_ms;

                            if (unit == "Days") {
                                converted_ms = Math.round(milliseconds / oneDay);
                            } else if (unit == "Hours") {
                                converted_ms = Math.round(milliseconds / oneHour);
                            } else if (unit == "Minutes") {
                                converted_ms = Math.round(milliseconds / oneMinute);
                            }

                            return converted_ms;
                        }

                        // reset the content to default
                        function showDefaultContent(defaultContent) {

                            $('li.christmas-countdown').addClass('free-delivery');
                            $('li.free-delivery').html(defaultContent);
                            $('li.free-delivery').removeClass('christmas-countdown');

                        }

                        // get days, hours or minutes as time unit for each language
                        function getTimeUnit(timeRemaining) {

                            var timeUnit = {
                                "en": {
                                    plural: "Days",
                                    single: "Day"
                                },
                                "fr": {
                                    plural: "Jours",
                                    single: "Jour"
                                },
                                "es": {
                                    plural: "Días",
                                    single: "Día"
                                },
                                "it": {
                                    plural: "Giorni",
                                    single: "Giorno"
                                },
                                "de": {
                                    plural: "Tage",
                                    single: "Tag"
                                },
                                "pt": {
                                    plural: "Dias",
                                    single: "Dia"
                                },
                                "ru": {
                                    plural: "Дней",
                                    single: "День"
                                },
                                "ja": {
                                    plural: "日",
                                    single: "日"
                                }
                            };

                            if (timeRemaining <= 86400000) {
                                // less than 1 day

                                var timeUnit = {
                                    "en": {
                                        plural: "Hours",
                                        single: "Hour"
                                    },
                                    "fr": {
                                        plural: "Heures",
                                        single: "Heures"
                                    },
                                    "es": {
                                        plural: "Horas",
                                        single: "Hora"
                                    },
                                    "it": {
                                        plural: "Ore",
                                        single: "Ora"
                                    },
                                    "de": {
                                        plural: "Stunden",
                                        single: "Stunde"
                                    },
                                    "pt": {
                                        plural: "Horas",
                                        single: "Hora"
                                    },
                                    "ru": {
                                        plural: "Часов",
                                        single: "Час"
                                    },
                                    "ja": {
                                        plural: "時間",
                                        single: "時間"
                                    }
                                };

                                if (timeRemaining <= 3600000) {
                                    // less than 1 hour

                                    var timeUnit = {
                                        "en": {
                                            plural: "Minutes",
                                            single: "Minute"
                                        },
                                        "fr": {
                                            plural: "Minutes",
                                            single: "Minute"
                                        },
                                        "es": {
                                            plural: "Minutos",
                                            single: "Minuto"
                                        },
                                        "it": {
                                            plural: "Minuti",
                                            single: "Minuto"
                                        },
                                        "de": {
                                            plural: "Minuten",
                                            single: "Minute"
                                        },
                                        "pt": {
                                            plural: "Minutos",
                                            single: "Minuto"
                                        },
                                        "ru": {
                                            plural: "Минут",
                                            single: "Минута"
                                        },
                                        "ja": {
                                            plural: "分",
                                            single: "分"
                                        }
                                    };

                                }
                            }

                            return timeUnit;

                        }

                        // function to update time amount and time unit content
                        function updateTimeRemainingContent(timeRemaining, content, lang) {

                            var $timeUnit = getTimeUnit(timeRemaining); // get time unit (Days/Hours/Minutes for all languages, plural and single)
                            var $daysLeft = convertTime(timeRemaining, 'Days'); // convert to days
                            var $hoursLeft = convertTime(timeRemaining, 'Hours'); // convert to hours
                            var $minutesLeft = convertTime(timeRemaining, 'Minutes'); // convert to minutes

                            //$('li.christmas-countdown').removeClass('trustpilot'); // remove TP styling
                            $('li.free-delivery').addClass('christmas-countdown'); // remove TP styling
                            $('li.christmas-countdown').removeClass('free-delivery'); // remove TP styling
                            $('li.christmas-countdown').html(content); // add in standard content
                            $('span.countdown-time').text($daysLeft); // add in number of days left

                            if (timeRemaining <= 259200000) {
                                // less than 3 days remaining
                                // console.log('less than 3 days remaining - change icon to red');// debugging - remove on production site

                                $('.countdown-time').addClass('red'); // change calendar to red

                                if ($timeUnit['en']['plural'] == 'Days') {
                                    // more than 1 day
                                    $('li.christmas-countdown strong.time-unit').text($timeUnit[lang]['plural']); // change time unit to days
                                    if ($daysLeft === 1) {
                                        $('li.christmas-countdown strong.time-unit').text($timeUnit[lang]['single']); // change time unit to day
                                    }

                                } else if ($timeUnit['en']['plural'] == 'Hours') {
                                    // less than 1 day
                                    // console.log('less than 1 day remaining - change unit to hours'); // debugging - remove on production site

                                    $('span.countdown-time').text($hoursLeft); // add number of hours left
                                    $('li.christmas-countdown strong.time-unit').text($timeUnit[lang]['plural']); // change time unit to days
                                    if ($hoursLeft === 1) {
                                        $('li.christmas-countdown strong.time-unit').text($timeUnit[lang]['single']); // change time unit to hour
                                    }

                                } else if ($timeUnit['en']['plural'] == 'Minutes') {
                                    // less than 1 hour
                                    // console.log('less than 1 hour remaining - change unit to minutes'); // debugging - remove on production site

                                    $('span.countdown-time').text($minutesLeft); // add number of minutes left
                                    $('li.christmas-countdown strong.time-unit').text($timeUnit[lang]['plural']); // change time unit to days
                                    if ($minutesLeft === 1) {
                                        $('li.christmas-countdown strong.time-unit').text($timeUnit[lang]['single']); // change time unit to minute
                                    }

                                }

                            }
                        }

                        //If last delivery date is on Saturday, Sunday or Monday set last day for delivery on Friday.

                        function isDeliveryOnWeekend(date) {

                            var day = date.getDay();

                            switch (day) {

                            case 6:

                                date.setDate(date.getDate() - 1);

                                break;

                            case 0:

                                date.setDate(date.getDate() - 2);

                                break;

                            case 1:

                                date.setDate(date.getDate() - 3);

                                break;

                            default:

                                break;

                            }

                            return date;

                        }



                        function updateCSS() {

                            if ($('ul.affirmations li').length > 3) {

                                $('ul.affirmations li:eq(0)').width('23%');

                                $('ul.affirmations li:eq(1)').width('30%');

                                $('ul.affirmations li:eq(2)').width('22%');

                                $('ul.affirmations li:eq(3)').width('25%');

                            }

                        }



                        var $countryCode = '';

                        function doChristmasCountdown(defaultContent) {

                            //console.log(getUrlParameter(date));

                            var $now = getUVServerTime(); // get today's date



                            if (getUVCountyCode()) {

                                // get country code from universal variable

                                $countryCode = getUVCountyCode();





                            } else // console.log('Country code from UV: ' + $countryCode);
                            {

                                // can't get UV so get country code from the selector instead

                                // console.log('Country code from locale picker');

                                $countryCode = $('#localpicker').getPickerCountryCode(); // get the country code     

                            }

                            // determine if user's country is in the json data

                            if ($.inArray($countryCode, $.fn.getJSONCountryCodes()) >= 0) {

                                // country is on the list



                                var data = christmasDeliveryData.countries;



                                $.each(christmasDeliveryData.countries, function(i, data) {

                                    //loop through each country



                                    if ($countryCode === data.country_code) {

                                        // get user's country

                                        // console.log('Country:' + data.country_code); // debugging - remove on production site

                                        // console.log('Language:' + data.language_code); // debugging - remove on production site



                                        var $standardContent = data.standard_delivery_content;

                                        var $expressContent = data.express_delivery_content;

                                        var $language = data.language_code;



                                        $.each(data.last_delivery_dates, function(i, date) {

                                            // loop through each last delivery date



                                            var $lastStandardDate = new Date(date.standard); // create date for last standard delivery

                                            var $lastExpressDate = new Date(date.express); // create date for last express delivery

                                            $lastStandardDate = isDeliveryOnWeekend($lastStandardDate);

                                            $lastExpressDate = isDeliveryOnWeekend($lastExpressDate);

                                            var $timeToStandardDelivery = getTimeBetween(new Date($now), $lastStandardDate); // get number of milliseconds left for standard delivery

                                            var $timeToExpressDelivery = getTimeBetween(new Date($now), $lastExpressDate); // get number of milliseconds left for express delivery

                                            // console.log('Last date for Standard deivery: ' + $lastStandardDate); // debugging - remove on production site

                                            // console.log('Last date for Express delivery: ' + $lastExpressDate); // debugging - remove on production site



                                            if ($timeToStandardDelivery > 0 || $timeToExpressDelivery > 0) {

                                                // standard or express delivery still possible

                                                // console.log('standard or express delivery still possible'); // debugging - remove on production site



                                                if ($timeToStandardDelivery <= 1728000000) {

                                                    // less than 20 days left for standard delivery

                                                    // TODO: refactor this section



                                                    if ($timeToStandardDelivery > 0) {

                                                        // standard delivery

                                                        // console.log('standard delivery - show standard delivery content'); // debugging - remove on production site

                                                        // update the content for standard delivery

                                                        updateTimeRemainingContent($timeToStandardDelivery, $standardContent, $language);



                                                    } else if ($timeToExpressDelivery > 0) {

                                                        // express delivery only

                                                        // console.log('express delivery only - show express delivery content'); // debugging - remove on production site

                                                        // update the content for express delivery

                                                        updateTimeRemainingContent($timeToExpressDelivery, $expressContent, $language);



                                                    }



                                                } else {

                                                    // console.log('more than 20 days - do not show countdown'); // debugging - remove on production site



                                                    showDefaultContent(defaultContent);



                                                }



                                            } else {

                                                // console.log('Christmas delivery has ended - show the default content'); // debugging - remove on production site



                                                showDefaultContent(defaultContent);



                                            }



                                        });

                                    }

                                });

                            }



                        }

                        // page load

                        $(document).ready(function() {



                            try {

                                var defaultContent = $('.free-delivery').html();

                                doChristmasCountdown(defaultContent);

                                updateCSS();



                            } catch (error) {

                                // console.log("Error with Christmas delivery coutdown: " + error); // debugging - remove on production site

                                callTrack('_trackEvent', 'JavaScript Error - Christmas Countdown ', 'Country: ' + $countryCode, 'Error: ' + error); // send event to Google Analytics



                                showDefaultContent(defaultContent);

                            }



                        });

                                                <div class="crcComponent crcPDPComponent crcPDPDescription" id="crcPDPComponentDescription">
                                                    <h2 class="from-description-field">Ragley Big AL 1.0 Hardtail Bike</h2>
                                                    <p>The Big AL is a versatile, playful and fun 29&quot;-wheeled hardtail trail riding bike with a strong and lightweight alloy frame with superb components to match. With modern geometry for an agile, stable and comfortable performance anywhere on the mountainside, this bike is also equipped with 140mm travel Marzocchi Bomber Z2 suspension forks and a Shimano Deore 1x11-Speed groupset. Plus, this groupset includes a wide-ranging 11-51 tooth cassette and Deore hydraulic disc brakes. And, this bike rolls upon Nukeproof Neutron Boost hubs, WTB ST i30 Tubeless Ready rims and Maxxis Minion tyres. And, it's armed with a Brand-X Ascend internally routed dropper seatpost.</p>
                                                    <p>The Big Al is the 29” counterpart to the Marley; designed as a fun all-rounder with the same performance and value that made its smaller-wheeled sibling a multiple test winner. </p>
                                                    <h3>Shimano Deore 11-Speed Groupset and Brand-X Dropper Seatpost</h3>
                                                    <p>The Big Al 1.0 takes all that’s great about the 2.0 but upgrades the spec: The addition of the group test winning Brand-X Ascend dropper plus the upgraded 11-speed Deore groupset and M6100 brakes. </p>
                                                    <h3>Marzocchi Z2 Rail 140mm Travel Suspension Forks</h3>
                                                    <p>Keeping things lively at the business end; a Marzocchi Z2 Rail provides additional stiffness with 140mm of exceptional damping to keep the front wheel digging into the dirt. </p>
                                                    <p>A perfect balance between all-out gravity-led tomfoolery and practical pedalability. Just like the Marley, the Big Al is well mannered during a leisurely all-day ride but drop the saddle and send it down the rough stuff for the good times… </p>
                                                    <p>Everything you could want from an all-round hardtail; get wild straight out of the box. </p>
                                                    <h3>Features:</h3>
                                                    <ul>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Frame: </strong>
                                                            Ragley Big Al - Alloy Boost 29&quot;
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Fork: </strong>
                                                            Marzocchi Bomber Z2, 140mm Travel, RAIL, Gloss Black, Kabolt:15x110, 1.5 Tapered steerer, 51mm offset 
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Headset: </strong>
                                                            Nukeproof Neutron ZS44/28.6 | ZS56/40 Headset with Ragley Top Cap
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Handlebar: </strong>
                                                            Ragley Alloy Handlebar, Black, 25mm Rise, 31.8mm Clamp (Width - S780mm, M780mm, L800mm, XL800mm)
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Stem: </strong>
                                                            Ragley 31.8mm clamp, 50mm length, +3&deg; rise
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Grips: </strong>
                                                            Ragley A20 Compound
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Front Wheel: </strong>
                                                            Nukeproof Neutron 15mm Boost Front Hub, WTB ST i30 TCS 2.0 29&quot; 32h rim
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Rear Wheel: </strong>
                                                            Nukeproof Neutron 148mm x 12mm Rear Hub, 36 points of engagement, HG Freehub, Sealed bearings, WTB ST i30 TCS 2.0 29&quot; 32h rim
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Thru Axle: </strong>
                                                            Length: 175mm, Pitch: M12*1.5, Thread length: 18mm
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Front Tyre: </strong>
                                                            Maxxis MINION DHF 29x2.5 WT 3C MaxxTerra/EXO+/TR 120TPI 
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Rear Tyre: </strong>
                                                            Maxxis MINION DHR II 29X2.40 WT 3C MaxxTerra/EXO/TR 60TPI 
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Rim Tape &amp; Valves: </strong>
                                                            32mm Tubeless Tape &amp; Tubeless tape supplied
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Chain: </strong>
                                                            11SPEED. W/QL, 118L
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Crankset: </strong>
                                                            Shimano Deore FC-M5100-1, 170MM, 30T
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Bottom Bracket: </strong>
                                                            Shimano Deore Hollowtech II 73mm BSA
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Front Brake: </strong>
                                                            Shimano Deore M6100, 180mm Rotor, Resin Pads
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Rear Brake: </strong>
                                                            Shimano Deore M6100, 180mm Rotor, Resin Pads
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Rear Derailleur: </strong>
                                                            Shimano Deore RD-M5100 SGS 11-SPEED, SHADOW PLUS DESIGN
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Rear Shifter: </strong>
                                                            Shimano Deore SL-M5100, 11-SPEED RAPIDFIRE, Direct attach to brake using iSpec EV
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Drivetrain Cables: </strong>
                                                            Shimano
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Cassette: </strong>
                                                            Shimano Deore M5100-11 11-13-15-18-21-24-28-33-39-45-51T
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Saddle: </strong>
                                                            Ragley Tracker Saddle
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Seat post: </strong>
                                                            Brand-X Ascend Internal Routed 31.6mm; MD - 150mm Drop; LG, XL - 170mm Drop
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Seat Clamp: </strong>
                                                            34.9mm Alloy
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>
                                                            <strong>Also included: </strong>
                                                            Ragley Chainstay protector, 5 Year Warranty and lifetime crash replacement, ISO 4210 Certified
                                                        </li>
                                                    </ul>
                                                    <h3>Easy Assembly</h3>
                                                    <p>When you order a bike, one of our trained mechanics will carefully prepare and pack your bike for shipping. Upon delivery, the assembly is simple and all necessary tools and plastic pedals are conveniently included in the box.</p>
                                                    <p>Depending on the delivery service and destination, bikes will either be delivered in a large or a small box. Below is a guide as to how your bike will arrive:</p>
                                                    <ul>
                                                        <li>All bikes for delivery within the UK and Republic of Ireland will be delivered in a large box, except for balance bikes and BMX bikes, which are always delivered in manufacturer’s boxes.</li>
                                                        <li>All bikes for delivery within the EU on a standard service will be delivered in a large box. If an express delivery option is chosen, your bike will be packed into a small box. Again, the exception is balance bikes and BMX bikes, which are always delivered in manufacturer’s boxes.</li>
                                                        <li>All bikes for worldwide delivery outside the EU will be delivered in small boxes.</li>
                                                    </ul>
                                                    <p>

                                                        <a href="http://media.chainreactioncycles.com/s7viewers/html5/VideoViewer.html?videoserverurl=http://media.chainreactioncycles.com/is/content/&amp;emailurl=http://media.chainreactioncycles.com/s7/emailFriend&amp;serverUrl=http://media.chainreactioncycles.com/is/image/&amp;config=Scene7SharedAssets/Universal%5FHTML5%5FVideo&amp;contenturl=http://media.chainreactioncycles.com/skins/&amp;asset=ChainReactionCycles/MTB%5FSmall%5FBox%5FAssembly" title="MTB Small Box Assembly" target="_blank">
                                                            <strong>SMALL BOX.</strong>
                                                        </a>
